import { h, ref, computed } from 'vue'

const count = ref(0)

setInterval(() => {
  count.value++
  console.log('计数器：', count.value)
}, 1000)

const colors = ['red','green','blue','orange','purple']
const colorIndex = ref(0)

// 使用 computed 计算当前样式
const style = computed(() => ({ color: colors[colorIndex.value] }))

// 每秒切换颜色
setInterval(() => {
  colorIndex.value = (colorIndex.value + 1) % colors.length
}, 1000)

div({style: style}) {
  p { 'Hello, OVS!' }
  p { count }
  p { '颜色变化演示' }
}

import { h, ref, computed } from 'vue'

const count = ref(0)

setInterval(() => {
  count.value++
  console.log('计数器：', count.value)
}, 1000)

const colors = ['red','green','blue','orange','purple']
const colorIndex = ref(0)

// 使用 computed 计算当前样式
const style = computed(() => ({ color: colors[colorIndex.value] }))

// 每秒切换颜色
setInterval(() => {
  colorIndex.value = (colorIndex.value + 1) % colors.length
}, 1000)

div({style: style}) {
  p { 'Hello, OVS!' }
  p { count }
  p { '颜色变化演示' }
}

import { h, ref, computed } from 'vue'

const count = ref(0)

setInterval(() => {
  count.value++
  console.log('计数器：', count.value)
}, 1000)

const colors = ['red','green','blue','orange','purple']
const colorIndex = ref(0)

// 使用 computed 计算当前样式
const style = computed(() => ({ color: colors[colorIndex.value] }))

// 每秒切换颜色
setInterval(() => {
  colorIndex.value = (colorIndex.value + 1) % colors.length
}, 1000)

div({style: style}) {
  p { 'Hello, OVS!' }
  p { count }
  p { '颜色变化演示' }
  
}

import { h, ref, computed } from 'vue'

const count = ref(0)

setInterval(() => {
  count.value++
  console.log('计数器：', count.value)
}, 1000)

const colors = ['red','green','blue','orange','purple']
const colorIndex = ref(0)

// 使用 computed 计算当前样式
const style = computed(() => ({ color: colors[colorIndex.value] }))

// 每秒切换颜色
setInterval(() => {
  colorIndex.value = (colorIndex.value + 1) % colors.length
}, 1000)

div({style: style}) {
  p { 'Hello, OVS!' }
  p { count }
  p { '颜色变化演示' }
  
}

[2025-10-30T12:49:51.539Z]
import { h, ref, computed } from 'vue'

const count = ref(0)

setInterval(() => {
  count.value++
  console.log('计数器：', count.value)
}, 1000)

const colors = ['red','green','blue','orange','purple']
const colorIndex = ref(0)

// 使用 computed 计算当前样式
const style = computed(() => ({ color: colors[colorIndex.value] }))

// 每秒切换颜色
setInterval(() => {
  colorIndex.value = (colorIndex.value + 1) % colors.length
}, 1000)

div({style: style}) {
  p { 'Hello, OVS!' }
  p { count }
  p { '颜色变化演示' }
  
}
================================================================================

[2025-10-30T12:49:51.540Z]
import {createReactiveVNode} from '../utils/ReactiveVNode';
import {h,ref,computed} from 'vue';
export default (function(){const count = ref(0);
const colors = ['red','green','blue','orange','purple',];
const colorIndex = ref(0);
const style = computed(() => ({color:colors[colorIndex.value],}));
const children = [];
setInterval(() => {count.value++;
console.log('计数器：',count.value);
},1000);
setInterval(() => {colorIndex.value = (colorIndex.value + 1) % colors.length;
},1000);
children.push(createReactiveVNode('div',{style:style,},[createReactiveVNode('p',{},['Hello, OVS!',]),createReactiveVNode('p',{},[count,]),createReactiveVNode('p',{},['颜色变化演示',]),]));
return children})()

import { h, ref, computed } from 'vue'

const count = ref(0)

setInterval(() => {
  count.value++
  console.log('计数器：', count.value)
}, 1000)

const colors = ['red','green','blue','orange','purple']
const colorIndex = ref(0)

// 使用 computed 计算当前样式
const style = computed(() => ({ color: colors[colorIndex.value] }))

// 每秒切换颜色
setInterval(() => {
  colorIndex.value = (colorIndex.value + 1) % colors.length
}, 1000)

div({style: style}) {
  p { 'Hello, OVS!' }
  p { count }
  p { '颜色变化演示' }
  
}

console.log('计数器：',count.value);
},1000);
setInterval(() => {colorIndex.value = (colorIndex.value + 1) % colors.length;
},1000);

import { h, ref, computed } from 'vue'

const count = ref(0)

setInterval(() => {
  count.value++
  console.log('计数器：', count.value)
}, 1000)

const colors = ['red','green','blue','orange','purple']
const colorIndex = ref(0)

// 使用 computed 计算当前样式
const style = computed(() => ({ color: colors[colorIndex.value] }))

// 每秒切换颜色
setInterval(() => {
  colorIndex.value = (colorIndex.value + 1) % colors.length
}, 1000)

div({style: style}) {
  p { 'Hello, OVS!' }
  p { count }
  p { '颜色变化演示' }
  
}

import {createReactiveVNode} from '../utils/ReactiveVNode';
import {h,ref,computed} from 'vue';
export default (function(){const count = ref(0);
const colors = ['red','green','blue','orange','purple',];
const colorIndex = ref(0);
const style = computed(() => ({color:colors[colorIndex.value],}));
const children = [];
setInterval(() => {count.value++;
console.log('计数器：',count.value);
},1000);
setInterval(() => {colorIndex.value = (colorIndex.value + 1) % colors.length;
},1000);
children.push(createReactiveVNode('div',{style:style,},[createReactiveVNode('p',{},['Hello, OVS!',]),createReactiveVNode('p',{},[count,]),createReactiveVNode('p',{},['颜色变化演示',]),]));
return children})()

import { h, ref, computed } from 'vue'

const count = ref(0)

setInterval(() => {
  count.value++
  console.log('计数器：', count.value)
}, 1000)

const colors = ['red','green','blue','orange','purple']
const colorIndex = ref(0)

// 使用 computed 计算当前样式
const style = computed(() => ({ color: colors[colorIndex.value] }))

// 每秒切换颜色
setInterval(() => {
  colorIndex.value = (colorIndex.value + 1) % colors.length
}, 1000)

div({style: style}) {
  p { 'Hello, OVS!' }
  p { count }
  p { '颜色变化演示' }
  
}
================================================================================

[2025-10-30T12:59:43.113Z]
import {createReactiveVNode} from '../utils/ReactiveVNode';
import {h,ref,computed} from 'vue';
export default (function(){const count = ref(0);
const colors = ['red','green','blue','orange','purple',];
const colorIndex = ref(0);
const style = computed(() => ({color:colors[colorIndex.value],}));
const children = [];
setInterval(() => {count.value++;
console.log('计数器：',count.value);
},1000);
setInterval(() => {colorIndex.value = (colorIndex.value + 1) % colors.length;
},1000);
children.push(createReactiveVNode('div',{style:style,},[createReactiveVNode('p',{},['Hello, OVS!',]),createReactiveVNode('p',{},[count,]),createReactiveVNode('p',{},['颜色变化演示',]),]));
return children})()

import { h, ref, computed } from 'vue'

const count = ref(0)

setInterval(() => {
  count.value++
  console.log('计数器：', count.value)
}, 1000)

const colors = ['red','green','blue','orange','purple']
const colorIndex = ref(0)

// 使用 computed 计算当前样式
const style = computed(() => ({ color: colors[colorIndex.value] }))

// 每秒切换颜色
setInterval(() => {
  colorIndex.value = (colorIndex.value + 1) % colors.length
}, 1000)

div({style: style}) {
  p { 'Hello, OVS!' }
  p { co }
  p { '颜色变化演示' }
  
}

import { h, ref, computed } from 'vue'

const count = ref(0)

setInterval(() => {
  count.value++
  console.log('计数器：', count.value)
}, 1000)

const colors = ['red','green','blue','orange','purple']
const colorIndex = ref(0)

// 使用 computed 计算当前样式
const style = computed(() => ({ color: colors[colorIndex.value] }))

// 每秒切换颜色
setInterval(() => {
  colorIndex.value = (colorIndex.value + 1) % colors.length
}, 1000)

div({style: style}) {
  p { 'Hello, OVS!' }
  p { co }
  p { '颜色变化演示' }
  
}
================================================================================

[2025-10-30T13:00:21.153Z]
import {createReactiveVNode} from '../utils/ReactiveVNode';
import {h,ref,computed} from 'vue';
export default (function(){const count = ref(0);
const colors = ['red','green','blue','orange','purple',];
const colorIndex = ref(0);
const style = computed(() => ({color:colors[colorIndex.value],}));
const children = [];
setInterval(() => {count.value++;
console.log('计数器：',count.value);
},1000);
setInterval(() => {colorIndex.value = (colorIndex.value + 1) % colors.length;
},1000);
children.push(createReactiveVNode('div',{style:style,},[createReactiveVNode('p',{},['Hello, OVS!',]),createReactiveVNode('p',{},[co,]),createReactiveVNode('p',{},['颜色变化演示',]),]));
return children})()

import { h, ref, computed } from 'vue'

const count = ref(0)

setInterval(() => {
  count.value++
  console.log('计数器：', count.value)
}, 1000)

const colors = ['red','green','blue','orange','purple']
const colorIndex = ref(0)

// 使用 computed 计算当前样式
const style = computed(() => ({ color: colors[colorIndex.value] }))

// 每秒切换颜色
setInterval(() => {
  colorIndex.value = (colorIndex.value + 1) % colors.length
}, 1000)

div({style: style}) {
  p { 'Hello, OVS!' }
  p { count }
  p { '颜色变化演示' }
  
}
================================================================================

[2025-10-30T13:35:57.044Z]
import {createReactiveVNode} from '../utils/ReactiveVNode';

import {h,ref,computed} from 'vue';
export default (function(){
  const count = ref(0);
  const colors = ['red','green','blue','orange','purple',];
  const colorIndex = ref(0);
  const style = computed(() => ({color:colors[colorIndex.value],}));
  const children = [];
  setInterval(() => {
    count.value++;
    console.log('计数器：',count.value);
  }
,1000);
  setInterval(() => {
    colorIndex.value = (colorIndex.value + 1) % colors.length;
  }
,1000);
  children.push(createReactiveVNode('div',{style:style,},[createReactiveVNode('p',{},['Hello, OVS!',]),createReactiveVNode('p',{},[count,]),createReactiveVNode('p',{},['颜色变化演示',]),]));
  return children}
)()

import { h, ref, computed } from 'vue'

const count = ref(0)

setInterval(() => {
  count.value++
  console.log('计数器：', count.value)
}, 1000)

const colors = ['red','green','blue','orange','purple']
const colorIndex = ref(0)

// 使用 computed 计算当前样式
const style = computed(() => ({ color: colors[colorIndex.value] }))

// 每秒切换颜色
setInterval(() => {
  colorIndex.value = (colorIndex.value + 1) % colors.length
}, 1000)

div({style: style}) {
  p { 'Hello, OVS!' }
  p { count }
  p { '颜色变化演示' }
  
}

[2025-10-30T17:51:26.646Z]
import {createReactiveVNode} from '../utils/ReactiveVNode';

import {h,ref,computed} from 'vue';
export default (function(){
  const count = ref(0);
  const colors = ['red','green','blue','orange','purple',];
  const colorIndex = ref(0);
  const style = computed(() => ({color:colors[colorIndex.value],}));
  const children = [];
  setInterval(() => {
    count.value++;
    console.log('计数器：',count.value);
  },1000);
  setInterval(() => {
    colorIndex.value = (colorIndex.value + 1) % colors.length;
  },1000);
  children.push(createReactiveVNode('div',{style:style,},[createReactiveVNode('p',{},['Hello, OVS!',]),createReactiveVNode('p',{},[count,]),createReactiveVNode('p',{},['颜色变化演示',]),]));
  return children})()

export function Button(state) {
  const { text, color } = state.props
  let finalColor = color || theme
  
  button {
    p { text + '/' + finalColor }
  }
}

  a {
    span { label }
  }
}

import {createReactiveVNode} from '../utils/ReactiveVNode';

const theme = 'blue';
export function Button(state){
  const {text,color} = state.props;
  let finalColor = color;
  createReactiveVNode('button',{},[createReactiveVNode('p',{},[text + '/' + finalColor,]),]);
}
export const Link = function(state){
  const {href,label} = state.props;
  createReactiveVNode('a',{},[createReactiveVNode('span',{},[label,]),]);
};
